Local Open Scope cat.

(**
The definition of a Street fibration of categories
 *)
Section StreetFibration.
  Context {E B : category}
          (F : E ⟶ B).

  Definition is_cartesian_sfib
             {e₁ e₂ : E}
             (f : e₁--> e₂)
    : UU
    := ∏ (z : E)
         (g : z --> e₂)
         (h : F z --> F e₁)
         (p : #F g = h · #F f),
       ∃! (φ : z --> e₁),
       #F φ = h
       ×
       φ · f = g.

  
E, B: category
F: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
isaprop (is_cartesian_sfib f)

  
E, B: category
F: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
isaprop (is_cartesian_sfib f)

    
E, B: category
F: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
t: E
t0: E ⟦ t, e₂ ⟧
t1: B ⟦ F t, F e₁ ⟧
t2: # F t0 = t1 · # F f
isofhlevel 1
  (∃! φ : E ⟦ t, e₁ ⟧, # F φ = t1 × φ · f = t0)

    apply isapropiscontr.
  Qed.

  Definition cartesian_factorization_sfib
             {e₁ e₂ : E}
             {f : e₁--> e₂}
             (Hf : is_cartesian_sfib f)
             {z : E}
             (g : z --> e₂)
             (h : F z --> F e₁)
             (p : #F g = h · #F f)
    : z --> e₁
    := pr11 (Hf z g h p).

  Definition cartesian_factorization_sfib_over
             {e₁ e₂ : E}
             {f : e₁--> e₂}
             (Hf : is_cartesian_sfib f)
             {z : E}
             (g : z --> e₂)
             (h : F z --> F e₁)
             (p : #F g = h · #F f)
    : #F (cartesian_factorization_sfib Hf g h p) = h
    := pr121 (Hf z g h p).

  Definition cartesian_factorization_sfib_commute
             {e₁ e₂ : E}
             {f : e₁--> e₂}
             (Hf : is_cartesian_sfib f)
             {z : E}
             (g : z --> e₂)
             (h : F z --> F e₁)
             (p : #F g = h · #F f)
    : cartesian_factorization_sfib Hf g h p · f = g
    := pr221 (Hf z g h p).

  
E, B: category
F: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
Hf: is_cartesian_sfib f
z: E
g: E ⟦ z, e₂ ⟧
h: B ⟦ F z, F e₁ ⟧
p: # F g = h · # F f
φ₁, φ₂: E ⟦ z, e₁ ⟧
p₁: # F φ₁ = h
p₂: # F φ₂ = h
q₁: φ₁ · f = g
q₂: φ₂ · f = g
φ₁ = φ₂

  
E, B: category
F: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
Hf: is_cartesian_sfib f
z: E
g: E ⟦ z, e₂ ⟧
h: B ⟦ F z, F e₁ ⟧
p: # F g = h · # F f
φ₁, φ₂: E ⟦ z, e₁ ⟧
p₁: # F φ₁ = h
p₂: # F φ₂ = h
q₁: φ₁ · f = g
q₂: φ₂ · f = g
φ₁ = φ₂

    exact (maponpaths
             pr1
             (proofirrelevance
                _
                (isapropifcontr (Hf z g h p))
                (φ₁ ,, p₁ ,, q₁)
                (φ₂ ,, p₂ ,, q₂))).
  Defined.

  Definition street_fib
    : UU
    := ∏ (e : E)
         (b : B)
         (f : b --> F e),
       ∑ (bb : E)
         (ff_i : bb --> e × z_iso (F bb) b),
       # F (pr1 ff_i) = pr2 ff_i · f
       ×
       is_cartesian_sfib (pr1 ff_i).
End StreetFibration.

(**
 *)

E, B: category
F: E ⟶ B
e: E
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, F e ⟧
bb₁, bb₂: E
ff₁: E ⟦ bb₁, e ⟧
β₁: z_iso (F bb₁) b
ff₂: E ⟦ bb₂, e ⟧
β₂: z_iso (F bb₂) b
over₁: # F ff₁ = β₁ · f
over₂: # F ff₂ = β₂ · f
cart₁: is_cartesian_sfib F ff₁
cart₂: is_cartesian_sfib F ff₂
E ⟦ bb₁, bb₂ ⟧


E, B: category
F: E ⟶ B
e: E
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, F e ⟧
bb₁, bb₂: E
ff₁: E ⟦ bb₁, e ⟧
β₁: z_iso (F bb₁) b
ff₂: E ⟦ bb₂, e ⟧
β₂: z_iso (F bb₂) b
over₁: # F ff₁ = β₁ · f
over₂: # F ff₂ = β₂ · f
cart₁: is_cartesian_sfib F ff₁
cart₂: is_cartesian_sfib F ff₂
E ⟦ bb₁, bb₂ ⟧

  
E, B: category
F: E ⟶ B
e: E
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, F e ⟧
bb₁, bb₂: E
ff₁: E ⟦ bb₁, e ⟧
β₁: z_iso (F bb₁) b
ff₂: E ⟦ bb₂, e ⟧
β₂: z_iso (F bb₂) b
over₁: # F ff₁ = β₁ · f
over₂: # F ff₂ = β₂ · f
cart₁: is_cartesian_sfib F ff₁
cart₂: is_cartesian_sfib F ff₂
# F ff₁ = β₁ · inv_from_z_iso β₂ · # F ff₂

  abstract
    (rewrite over₁, over₂ ;
     rewrite !assoc' ;
     apply maponpaths ;
     rewrite !assoc ;
     rewrite z_iso_after_z_iso_inv ;
     rewrite id_left ;
     apply idpath).
Defined.

Section UniqueLifts.
  Context {E B : category}
          (F : E ⟶ B)
          {e : E}
          {b : B}
          (f : b --> F e)
          (bb₁ bb₂ : E)
          (ff₁ : bb₁ --> e)
          (β₁ : z_iso (F bb₁) b)
          (ff₂ : bb₂ --> e)
          (β₂ : z_iso (F bb₂) b)
          (over₁ : # F (ff₁) = β₁ · f)
          (over₂ : # F (ff₂) = β₂ · f)
          (cart₁ : is_cartesian_sfib F ff₁)
          (cart₂ : is_cartesian_sfib F ff₂).

  Let ζ : bb₁ --> bb₂
    := lift_unique_sfib_map F f bb₁ bb₂ ff₁ β₁ ff₂ β₂ over₁ over₂ cart₁ cart₂.
  Let ζinv : bb₂ --> bb₁
    := lift_unique_sfib_map F f bb₂ bb₁ ff₂ β₂ ff₁ β₁ over₂ over₁ cart₂ cart₁.

  
E, B: category
F: E ⟶ B
e: E
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, F e ⟧
bb₁, bb₂: E
ff₁: E ⟦ bb₁, e ⟧
β₁: z_iso (F bb₁) b
ff₂: E ⟦ bb₂, e ⟧
β₂: z_iso (F bb₂) b
over₁: # F ff₁ = β₁ · f
over₂: # F ff₂ = β₂ · f
cart₁: is_cartesian_sfib F ff₁
cart₂: is_cartesian_sfib F ff₂
ζ:= lift_unique_sfib_map F f bb₁ bb₂ ff₁ β₁ ff₂ β₂
  over₁ over₂ cart₁ cart₂: E ⟦ bb₁, bb₂ ⟧
ζinv:= lift_unique_sfib_map F f bb₂ bb₁ ff₂ β₂ ff₁ β₁
  over₂ over₁ cart₂ cart₁: E ⟦ bb₂, bb₁ ⟧
ζ · ζinv = identity bb₁

ζ:= lift_unique_sfib_map F f bb₁ bb₂ ff₁ β₁ ff₂ β₂
  over₁ over₂ cart₁ cart₂: E ⟦ bb₁, bb₂ ⟧
ζinv:= lift_unique_sfib_map F f bb₂ bb₁ ff₂ β₂ ff₁ β₁
  over₂ over₁ cart₂ cart₁: E ⟦ bb₂, bb₁ ⟧
β₁ · (inv_from_z_iso β₂ · (β₂ · inv_from_z_iso β₁)) =
identity (F bb₁)

  over₁ over₂ cart₁ cart₂: E ⟦ bb₁, bb₂ ⟧

  over₂ over₁ cart₂ cart₁: E ⟦ bb₂, bb₁ ⟧
# F
  (cartesian_factorization_sfib F cart₁ ff₂
     (β₂ · inv_from_z_iso β₁)
     (lift_unique_sfib_map_subproof E B F e b f bb₂
        bb₁ ff₂ β₂ ff₁ β₁ over₂ over₁))
· # F
    (cartesian_factorization_sfib F cart₂ ff₁
       (β₁ · inv_from_z_iso β₂)
       (lift_unique_sfib_map_subproof E B F e b f bb₁
          bb₂ ff₁ β₁ ff₂ β₂ over₁ over₂)) =
identity (F bb₂)

      
E, B: category
F: E ⟶ B
e: E
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, F e ⟧
bb₁, bb₂: E
ff₁: E ⟦ bb₁, e ⟧
β₁: z_iso (F bb₁) b
ff₂: E ⟦ bb₂, e ⟧
β₂: z_iso (F bb₂) b
over₁: # F ff₁ = β₁ · f
over₂: # F ff₂ = β₂ · f
cart₁: is_cartesian_sfib F ff₁
cart₂: is_cartesian_sfib F ff₂
ζ:= lift_unique_sfib_map F f bb₁ bb₂ ff₁ β₁ ff₂ β₂
  over₁ over₂ cart₁ cart₂: E ⟦ bb₁, bb₂ ⟧
ζinv:= lift_unique_sfib_map F f bb₂ bb₁ ff₂ β₂ ff₁ β₁
  over₂ over₁ cart₂ cart₁: E ⟦ bb₂, bb₁ ⟧
β₂ · inv_from_z_iso β₁ · (β₁ · inv_from_z_iso β₂) =
identity (F bb₂)

(**
The projection of a fibration is a Street fibration
 *)
Section CleavingToStreetFib.
  Context {B : category}
          {D : disp_cat B}.

  Let E : category := total_category D.
  Let P : E ⟶ B := pr1_category D.

  
B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_cartesian (pr2 f)
z: E
g: E ⟦ z, e₂ ⟧
h: B ⟦ P z, P e₁ ⟧
p: # P g = h · # P f
isaprop (∑ φ : E ⟦ z, e₁ ⟧, # P φ = h × φ · f = g)

  
B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_cartesian (pr2 f)
z: E
g: E ⟦ z, e₂ ⟧
h: B ⟦ P z, P e₁ ⟧
p: # P g = h · # P f
isaprop (∑ φ : E ⟦ z, e₁ ⟧, # P φ = h × φ · f = g)

    
B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_cartesian (pr2 f)
z: E
g: E ⟦ z, e₂ ⟧
h: B ⟦ P z, P e₁ ⟧
p: # P g = h · # P f
lift:= H (pr1 z) h (pr2 z)
(transportf (λ z0 : B ⟦ P z, P e₂ ⟧, pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₂) p (pr2 g)): ∃! gg : pr2 z -->[ h] pr2 e₁,
(gg ;; pr2 f)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ P z, P e₂ ⟧,
   pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₂) p 
  (pr2 g)
isaprop (∑ φ : E ⟦ z, e₁ ⟧, # P φ = h × φ · f = g)

    
B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_cartesian (pr2 f)
z: E
g: E ⟦ z, e₂ ⟧
h: B ⟦ P z, P e₁ ⟧
p: # P g = h · # P f
lift:= H (pr1 z) h (pr2 z)
(transportf (λ z0 : B ⟦ P z, P e₂ ⟧, pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₂) p (pr2 g)): ∃! gg : pr2 z -->[ h] pr2 e₁,
(gg ;; pr2 f)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ P z, P e₂ ⟧,
   pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₂) p 
  (pr2 g)
isProofIrrelevant
  (∑ φ : E ⟦ z, e₁ ⟧, # P φ = h × φ · f = g)

    
B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_cartesian (pr2 f)
z: E
g: E ⟦ z, e₂ ⟧
h: B ⟦ P z, P e₁ ⟧
p: # P g = h · # P f
lift:= H (pr1 z) h (pr2 z)
(transportf (λ z0 : B ⟦ P z, P e₂ ⟧, pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₂) p (pr2 g)): ∃! gg : pr2 z -->[ h] pr2 e₁,
(gg ;; pr2 f)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ P z, P e₂ ⟧,
   pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₂) p 
  (pr2 g)
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ φ : E ⟦ z, e₁ ⟧, # P φ = h × φ · f = g
φ₁ = φ₂

   pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₂) p 
  (pr2 g)
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ φ : E ⟦ z, e₁ ⟧, # P φ = h × φ · f = g
φφ₁:= transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 z, pr1 e₁ ⟧,
   pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₁) 
  (pr12 φ₁) (pr21 φ₁): pr2 z -->[ h] pr2 e₁
φφ₂:= transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 z, pr1 e₁ ⟧,
   pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₁) 
  (pr12 φ₂) (pr21 φ₂): pr2 z -->[ h] pr2 e₁
transportf (mor_disp (pr2 z) (pr2 e₂))
  (cancel_postcomposition (pr11 φ₁) h (pr1 f)
     (pr12 φ₁)) (pr21 φ₁ ;; pr2 f)%mor_disp = ?b

  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 z, pr1 e₁ ⟧,
   pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₁) 
  (pr12 φ₂) (pr21 φ₂): pr2 z -->[ h] pr2 e₁
H₁: (φφ₁ ;; pr2 f)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ w : B ⟦ pr1 z, pr1 e₂ ⟧,
   pr2 z -->[ w] pr2 e₂) p 
  (pr2 g)
?b =
transportf
  (λ w : B ⟦ pr1 z, pr1 e₂ ⟧, pr2 z -->[ w] pr2 e₂) p
  (pr2 g)

   transportf
     (λ z0 : B ⟦ P z, P e₂ ⟧, pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₂)
     p (pr2 g)) (isapropifcontr lift): isProofIrrelevant
  (∑ gg : pr2 z -->[ h] pr2 e₁,
   (gg ;; pr2 f)%mor_disp =
   transportf
     (λ z0 : B ⟦ P z, P e₂ ⟧,
      pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₂) p 
     (pr2 g))
r: transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 z, pr1 e₁ ⟧,
   pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₁) 
  (pr12 φ₁) (pr21 φ₁) =
transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ pr1 z, pr1 e₁ ⟧,
   pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₁) 
  (pr12 φ₂) (pr21 φ₂)
transportf (mor_disp (pr2 z) (pr2 e₁))
  (pr12 φ₁ @ ! pr12 φ₂) (pr21 φ₁) = pr21 φ₂

 exact (is_cartesian_to_unique_sfib f H g h p).
    
B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_cartesian (pr2 f)
z: E
g: E ⟦ z, e₂ ⟧
h: B ⟦ P z, P e₁ ⟧
p: # P g = h · # P f
lift:= H (pr1 z) h (pr2 z)
(transportf (λ z0 : B ⟦ P z, P e₂ ⟧, pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₂) p (pr2 g)): ∃! gg : pr2 z -->[ h] pr2 e₁,
(gg ;; pr2 f)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ P z, P e₂ ⟧,
   pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₂) p 
  (pr2 g)
∑ φ : E ⟦ z, e₁ ⟧, # P φ = h × φ · f = g
 
B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_cartesian (pr2 f)
z: E
g: E ⟦ z, e₂ ⟧
h: B ⟦ P z, P e₁ ⟧
p: # P g = h · # P f
lift:= H (pr1 z) h (pr2 z)
(transportf (λ z0 : B ⟦ P z, P e₂ ⟧, pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₂) p (pr2 g)): ∃! gg : pr2 z -->[ h] pr2 e₁,
(gg ;; pr2 f)%mor_disp =
transportf
  (λ z0 : B ⟦ P z, P e₂ ⟧,
   pr2 z -->[ z0] pr2 e₂) p 
  (pr2 g)
h · pr1 f,, (pr11 lift ;; pr2 f)%mor_disp = g

      abstract
        (pose (pr21 lift) as q ; cbn in q ;
         use total2_paths_f ;
         [ exact (!p)
         | cbn ;
           rewrite q ;
           rewrite transport_f_f ;
           apply transportf_set ;
           apply homset_property ]).
  Defined.

gf: zz -->[ g · pr1 f] pr2 e₂
isaprop
  (∑ gg : zz -->[ g] pr2 e₁,
   (gg ;; pr2 f)%mor_disp = gf)

g: B ⟦ z, pr1 e₁ ⟧
zz: D z
gf: zz -->[ g · pr1 f] pr2 e₂
lift:= H (z,, zz) (g · pr1 f,, gf) g (idpath (# P (g · pr1 f,, gf))): ∃! φ : E ⟦ z,, zz, e₁ ⟧,
# P φ = g × φ · f = g · pr1 f,, gf
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ gg : zz -->[ g] pr2 e₁,
(gg ;; pr2 f)%mor_disp = gf
φφ₁:= g,, pr1 φ₁ : E ⟦ z,, zz, e₁ ⟧: E ⟦ z,, zz, e₁ ⟧
H₁: # P φφ₁ = g × φφ₁ · f = g · pr1 f,, gf
φφ₂:= g,, pr1 φ₂ : E ⟦ z,, zz, e₁ ⟧: E ⟦ z,, zz, e₁ ⟧
g = g

B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_cartesian_sfib P f
z: B
g: B ⟦ z, pr1 e₁ ⟧
zz: D z
gf: zz -->[ g · pr1 f] pr2 e₂
lift:= H (z,, zz) (g · pr1 f,, gf) g (idpath (# P (g · pr1 f,, gf))): ∃! φ : E ⟦ z,, zz, e₁ ⟧,
# P φ = g × φ · f = g · pr1 f,, gf
(λ gg : zz -->[ g] pr2 e₁, (gg ;; pr2 f)%mor_disp = gf)
  (transportf
     (λ z0 : B ⟦ P (z,, zz), P e₁ ⟧,
      pr2 (z,, zz) -->[ z0] pr2 e₁) (pr121 lift)
     (pr211 lift))
 abstract
          (simpl ;
           pose (transportb_transpose_right (fiber_paths (pr221 lift))) as p ;
           rewrite mor_disp_transportf_postwhisker ;
           cbn in p ;
           refine (maponpaths _ p @ _) ;
           unfold transportb ;
           rewrite transport_f_f ;
           apply transportf_set ;
           apply homset_property).
  Defined.

B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
HD: cleaving D
e: total_category D
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, pr1_category D e ⟧
∑ (bb : total_category D)
(ff_i : total_category D ⟦ bb, e ⟧
        × z_iso (pr1_category D bb) b),
# (pr1_category D) (pr1 ff_i) = pr2 ff_i · f
× is_cartesian_sfib (pr1_category D) (pr1 ff_i)

D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
HD: cleaving D
e: total_category D
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, pr1_category D e ⟧
c:= HD (pr1 e) b f (pr2 e): cartesian_lift (pr2 e) f
is_cartesian_sfib (pr1_category D) (f,, pr12 c)

    
B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
HD: cleaving D
e: total_category D
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, pr1_category D e ⟧
c:= HD (pr1 e) b f (pr2 e): cartesian_lift (pr2 e) f
f = identity b · f
 apply (!(id_left _)).
    
B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
HD: cleaving D
e: total_category D
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, pr1_category D e ⟧
c:= HD (pr1 e) b f (pr2 e): cartesian_lift (pr2 e) f
is_cartesian_sfib (pr1_category D) (f,, pr12 c)
 
B: category
D: disp_cat B
E:= total_category D: category
P:= pr1_category D: E ⟶ B
HD: cleaving D
e: total_category D
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, pr1_category D e ⟧
c:= HD (pr1 e) b f (pr2 e): cartesian_lift (pr2 e) f
is_cartesian (pr2 (f,, pr12 c))

      exact (pr22 c).
  Defined.
End CleavingToStreetFib.

(** Morphisms between Street fibrations *)
Definition preserves_cartesian
           {B₁ B₂ E₁ E₂ : category}
           (P₁ : E₁ ⟶ B₁)
           (P₂ : E₂ ⟶ B₂)
           (FE : E₁ ⟶ E₂)
  : UU
  := ∏ (e₁ e₂ : E₁)
       (f : e₁ --> e₂),
     is_cartesian_sfib P₁ f
     →
     is_cartesian_sfib P₂ (#FE f).


B, E: category
P: E ⟶ B
preserves_cartesian P P (functor_identity E)


B, E: category
P: E ⟶ B
preserves_cartesian P P (functor_identity E)

  
B, E: category
P: E ⟶ B
e₁, e₂: E
f: E ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_cartesian_sfib P f
is_cartesian_sfib P (# (functor_identity E) f)

  exact H.
Qed.


B₁, B₂, B₃, E₁, E₂, E₃: category
P₁: E₁ ⟶ B₁
P₂: E₂ ⟶ B₂
P₃: E₃ ⟶ B₃
FE₁: E₁ ⟶ E₂
FE₂: E₂ ⟶ E₃
HFE₁: preserves_cartesian P₁ P₂ FE₁
HFE₂: preserves_cartesian P₂ P₃ FE₂
preserves_cartesian P₁ P₃ (FE₁ ∙ FE₂)


B₁, B₂, B₃, E₁, E₂, E₃: category
P₁: E₁ ⟶ B₁
P₂: E₂ ⟶ B₂
P₃: E₃ ⟶ B₃

FE₂: E₂ ⟶ E₃
HFE₁: preserves_cartesian P₁ P₂ FE₁
HFE₂: preserves_cartesian P₂ P₃ FE₂
preserves_cartesian P₁ P₃ (FE₁ ∙ FE₂)

  
B₁, B₂, B₃, E₁, E₂, E₃: category
P₁: E₁ ⟶ B₁
P₂: E₂ ⟶ B₂
P₃: E₃ ⟶ B₃
FE₁: E₁ ⟶ E₂
FE₂: E₂ ⟶ E₃

HFE₂: preserves_cartesian P₂ P₃ FE₂
e₁, e₂: E₁
f: E₁ ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_cartesian_sfib P₁ f
is_cartesian_sfib P₃ (# (FE₁ ∙ FE₂) f)

  
B₁, B₂, B₃, E₁, E₂, E₃: category
P₁: E₁ ⟶ B₁
P₂: E₂ ⟶ B₂
P₃: E₃ ⟶ B₃

HFE₂: preserves_cartesian P₂ P₃ FE₂
e₁, e₂: E₁

H: is_cartesian_sfib P₁ f
is_cartesian_sfib P₂ (# FE₁ f)

  
B₁, B₂, B₃, E₁, E₂, E₃: category
P₁: E₁ ⟶ B₁
P₂: E₂ ⟶ B₂
P₃: E₃ ⟶ B₃
FE₁: E₁ ⟶ E₂
FE₂: E₂ ⟶ E₃

HFE₂: preserves_cartesian P₂ P₃ FE₂
e₁, e₂: E₁
f: E₁ ⟦ e₁, e₂ ⟧
H: is_cartesian_sfib P₁ f
is_cartesian_sfib P₁ f

  exact H.
Qed.


B₁, B₂, E₁, E₂: category
P₁: E₁ ⟶ B₁
P₂: E₂ ⟶ B₂
FE: E₁ ⟶ E₂
isaprop (preserves_cartesian P₁ P₂ FE)


B₁, B₂, E₁, E₂: category
P₁: E₁ ⟶ B₁
P₂: E₂ ⟶ B₂
FE: E₁ ⟶ E₂
isaprop (preserves_cartesian P₁ P₂ FE)

  
B₁, B₂, E₁, E₂: category
P₁: E₁ ⟶ B₁
P₂: E₂ ⟶ B₂
FE: E₁ ⟶ E₂
t, t0: E₁
t1: E₁ ⟦ t, t0 ⟧
t2: is_cartesian_sfib P₁ t1
isofhlevel 1
  ((λ _ : is_cartesian_sfib P₁ t1,
    is_cartesian_sfib P₂ (# FE t1)) t2)

  apply isaprop_is_cartesian_sfib.
Qed.

Definition mor_of_street_fib
           {B₁ B₂ E₁ E₂ : category}
           (P₁ : E₁ ⟶ B₁)
           (P₂ : E₂ ⟶ B₂)
  : UU
  := ∑ (FB : B₁ ⟶ B₂)
       (FE : E₁ ⟶ E₂),
     preserves_cartesian P₁ P₂ FE
     ×
     nat_z_iso (P₁ ∙ FB) (FE ∙ P₂).

Definition mor_of_street_fib_base
           {B₁ B₂ E₁ E₂ : category}
           {P₁ : E₁ ⟶ B₁}
           {P₂ : E₂ ⟶ B₂}
           (F : mor_of_street_fib P₁ P₂)
  : B₁ ⟶ B₂
  := pr1 F.

Definition mor_of_street_fib_total
           {B₁ B₂ E₁ E₂ : category}
           {P₁ : E₁ ⟶ B₁}
           {P₂ : E₂ ⟶ B₂}
           (F : mor_of_street_fib P₁ P₂)
  : E₁ ⟶ E₂
  := pr12 F.

Definition mor_of_street_fib_preserves_cartesian
           {B₁ B₂ E₁ E₂ : category}
           {P₁ : E₁ ⟶ B₁}
           {P₂ : E₂ ⟶ B₂}
           (F : mor_of_street_fib P₁ P₂)
  : preserves_cartesian P₁ P₂ (mor_of_street_fib_total F)
  := pr122 F.

Definition mor_of_street_fib_preserves_nat_z_iso
           {B₁ B₂ E₁ E₂ : category}
           {P₁ : E₁ ⟶ B₁}
           {P₂ : E₂ ⟶ B₂}
           (F : mor_of_street_fib P₁ P₂)
  : nat_z_iso
      (P₁ ∙ mor_of_street_fib_base F)
      (mor_of_street_fib_total F ∙ P₂)
  := pr222 F.


B, E: category
P: E ⟶ B
P ∙ functor_identity B ⟹ functor_identity E ∙ P

P: E ⟶ B
P ∙ functor_identity B ⟹ functor_identity E ∙ P

nat_trans_data (P ∙ functor_identity B)
  (functor_identity E ∙ P)

is_nat_trans (P ∙ functor_identity B)
  (functor_identity E ∙ P) ?t

nat_trans_data (P ∙ functor_identity B)
  (functor_identity E ∙ P)
 exact (λ _, identity _).

P: E ⟶ B
is_nat_trans (P ∙ functor_identity B)
  (functor_identity E ∙ P)
  (λ x : E, identity ((P ∙ functor_identity B) x))
 abstract
      (intros ? ? ? ;
       cbn ;
       rewrite id_left, id_right ;
       apply idpath).
Defined.

  (functor_identity E ∙ P)

  (functor_identity E ∙ P)

P ∙ functor_identity B ⟹ functor_identity E ∙ P

P: E ⟶ B

P: E ⟶ B
P ∙ functor_identity B ⟹ functor_identity E ∙ P
 exact (id_mor_of_street_fib_nat_trans P).
  
B, E: category
P: E ⟶ B
is_nat_z_iso (id_mor_of_street_fib_nat_trans P)
 
B, E: category
P: E ⟶ B
x: E
is_z_isomorphism (id_mor_of_street_fib_nat_trans P x)

    
B, E: category
P: E ⟶ B
x: E
is_z_isomorphism (identity (P x))

    apply identity_is_z_iso.
Defined.

Definition id_mor_of_street_fib
           {B E : category}
           (P : E ⟶ B)
  : mor_of_street_fib P P
  := functor_identity _
     ,,
     functor_identity _
     ,,
     identity_preserves_cartesian _
     ,,
     id_mor_of_street_fib_nat_z_iso P.


B₁, B₂, B₃, E₁, E₂, E₃: category
P₁: E₁ ⟶ B₁
P₂: E₂ ⟶ B₂
P₃: E₃ ⟶ B₃
F₁: mor_of_street_fib P₁ P₂
F₂: mor_of_street_fib P₂ P₃
P₁
∙ (mor_of_street_fib_base F₁
   ∙ mor_of_street_fib_base F₂)
⟹ (mor_of_street_fib_total F₁
   ∙ mor_of_street_fib_total F₂) ∙ P₃

      ∙ mor_of_street_fib_base F₂))
  ((mor_of_street_fib_total F₁
    ∙ mor_of_street_fib_total F₂) ∙ P₃)
 exact (λ x, #(mor_of_street_fib_base F₂) (mor_of_street_fib_preserves_nat_z_iso F₁ x)
                ·
                mor_of_street_fib_preserves_nat_z_iso F₂ _).
  
B₁, B₂, B₃, E₁, E₂, E₃: category
P₁: E₁ ⟶ B₁
P₂: E₂ ⟶ B₂
P₃: E₃ ⟶ B₃
F₁: mor_of_street_fib P₁ P₂
F₂: mor_of_street_fib P₂ P₃
is_nat_trans
  (P₁
   ∙ (mor_of_street_fib_base F₁
      ∙ mor_of_street_fib_base F₂))
  ((mor_of_street_fib_total F₁
    ∙ mor_of_street_fib_total F₂) ∙ P₃)
  (λ x : E₁,
   # (mor_of_street_fib_base F₂)
     (mor_of_street_fib_preserves_nat_z_iso F₁ x)
   · mor_of_street_fib_preserves_nat_z_iso F₂
       (mor_of_street_fib_total F₁ x))
 abstract
      (intros x y f ;
       cbn ;
       rewrite !assoc ;
       rewrite <- functor_comp ;
       etrans ;
         [ apply maponpaths_2 ;
           apply maponpaths ;
           exact (nat_trans_ax (mor_of_street_fib_preserves_nat_z_iso F₁) _ _ f)
         | ] ;
       rewrite functor_comp ;
       rewrite !assoc' ;
       apply maponpaths ;
       apply (nat_trans_ax (mor_of_street_fib_preserves_nat_z_iso F₂))).
Defined.

    ∙ mor_of_street_fib_total F₂) ∙ P₃)

     (mor_of_street_fib_total F₁ x))

Definition comp_mor_of_street_fib
           {B₁ B₂ B₃ E₁ E₂ E₃ : category}
           {P₁ : E₁ ⟶ B₁}
           {P₂ : E₂ ⟶ B₂}
           {P₃ : E₃ ⟶ B₃}
           (F₁ : mor_of_street_fib P₁ P₂)
           (F₂ : mor_of_street_fib P₂ P₃)
  : mor_of_street_fib P₁ P₃
  := mor_of_street_fib_base F₁ ∙ mor_of_street_fib_base F₂
     ,,
     mor_of_street_fib_total F₁ ∙ mor_of_street_fib_total F₂
     ,,
     composition_preserves_cartesian
       (mor_of_street_fib_preserves_cartesian F₁)
       (mor_of_street_fib_preserves_cartesian F₂)
     ,,
     comp_mor_of_street_fib_nat_z_iso F₁ F₂.

(** The type of Street fibrations is a proposition *)

B, E: category
HE: is_univalent E
F: E ⟶ B
isaprop (street_fib F)


B, E: category
HE: is_univalent E
F: E ⟶ B
isaprop (street_fib F)

  
B, E: category
HE: is_univalent E
F: E ⟶ B
e: E
isofhlevel 1
  ((λ t : E,
    ∏ (b : B) (f : B ⟦ b, F t ⟧),
    ∑ (bb : E) (ff_i : E ⟦ bb, t ⟧ × z_iso (F bb) b),
    # F (pr1 ff_i) = pr2 ff_i · f
    × is_cartesian_sfib F (pr1 ff_i)) e)

  
B, E: category
HE: is_univalent E
F: E ⟶ B
e: E
b: B
isofhlevel 1
  ((λ t : B,
    ∏ f : B ⟦ t, F e ⟧,
    ∑ (bb : E) (ff_i : E ⟦ bb, e ⟧ × z_iso (F bb) t),
    # F (pr1 ff_i) = pr2 ff_i · f
    × is_cartesian_sfib F (pr1 ff_i)) b)

  
B, E: category
HE: is_univalent E
F: E ⟶ B
e: E
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, F e ⟧

· pr121 (pr2 φ₁) = ?b
B, E: category
HE: is_univalent E
F: E ⟶ B
e: E
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, F e ⟧
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ (bb : E) (ff_i : E ⟦ bb, e ⟧ × z_iso (F bb) b),
# F (pr1 ff_i) = pr2 ff_i · f
× is_cartesian_sfib F (pr1 ff_i)
?b = pr121 (pr2 φ₂)

      
B, E: category
HE: is_univalent E
F: E ⟶ B
e: E
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, F e ⟧
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ (bb : E) (ff_i : E ⟦ bb, e ⟧ × z_iso (F bb) b),
# F (pr1 ff_i) = pr2 ff_i · f
× is_cartesian_sfib F (pr1 ff_i)
# F
  (lift_unique_sfib_map F f (pr1 φ₂) (pr1 φ₁)
     (pr112 φ₂) (pr212 φ₂) (pr112 φ₁) (pr212 φ₁)
     (pr122 φ₂) (pr122 φ₁) (pr222 φ₂) (pr222 φ₁))
· pr121 (pr2 φ₁) = ?b

        
B, E: category
HE: is_univalent E
F: E ⟶ B
e: E
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, F e ⟧
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ (bb : E) (ff_i : E ⟦ bb, e ⟧ × z_iso (F bb) b),
# F (pr1 ff_i) = pr2 ff_i · f
× is_cartesian_sfib F (pr1 ff_i)
# F
  (lift_unique_sfib_map F f (pr1 φ₂) (pr1 φ₁)
     (pr112 φ₂) (pr212 φ₂) (pr112 φ₁) (pr212 φ₁)
     (pr122 φ₂) (pr122 φ₁) (pr222 φ₂) (pr222 φ₁)) =
?y'

        apply cartesian_factorization_sfib_over.
      
B, E: category
HE: is_univalent E
F: E ⟶ B
e: E
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, F e ⟧
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ (bb : E) (ff_i : E ⟦ bb, e ⟧ × z_iso (F bb) b),
# F (pr1 ff_i) = pr2 ff_i · f
× is_cartesian_sfib F (pr1 ff_i)
pr212 φ₂ · inv_from_z_iso (pr212 φ₁) · pr121 (pr2 φ₁) =
pr121 (pr2 φ₂)

      
B, E: category
HE: is_univalent E
F: E ⟶ B
e: E
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, F e ⟧
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ (bb : E) (ff_i : E ⟦ bb, e ⟧ × z_iso (F bb) b),
# F (pr1 ff_i) = pr2 ff_i · f
× is_cartesian_sfib F (pr1 ff_i)
pr212 φ₂
· (inv_from_z_iso (pr212 φ₁) · pr121 (pr2 φ₁)) =
pr121 (pr2 φ₂)

      
B, E: category
HE: is_univalent E
F: E ⟶ B
e: E
b: B
f: B ⟦ b, F e ⟧
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ (bb : E) (ff_i : E ⟦ bb, e ⟧ × z_iso (F bb) b),
# F (pr1 ff_i) = pr2 ff_i · f
× is_cartesian_sfib F (pr1 ff_i)
pr212 φ₂ · identity b = pr121 (pr2 φ₂)

      apply id_right.
Qed.

(**

C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂: C₁

p: f₁ = f₂
Hf₁: is_cartesian_sfib F f₁
is_cartesian_sfib F f₂

is_cartesian_sfib F f₁

  exact Hf₁.
Defined.

∃! φ : C₁ ⟦ w, x₁ ⟧, # F φ = h × φ · i = g

C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂: C₁
i: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hi: is_z_isomorphism i

w: C₁
g: C₁ ⟦ w, x₂ ⟧
h: C₂ ⟦ F w, F x₁ ⟧
p: # F g = h · # F i
isaprop (∑ φ : C₁ ⟦ w, x₁ ⟧, # F φ = h × φ · i = g)
 abstract
      (use invproofirrelevance ;
       intros φ₁ φ₂ ;
       use subtypePath ; [ intro ; apply isapropdirprod ; apply homset_property | ] ;
       refine (!(id_right _) @ _ @ id_right _) ;
       rewrite <- (z_iso_inv_after_z_iso i_iso) ;
       cbn ;
       rewrite !assoc ;
       rewrite (pr22 φ₁), (pr22 φ₂) ;
       apply idpath).

∑ φ : C₁ ⟦ w, x₁ ⟧, # F φ = h × φ · i = g

C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂: C₁
i: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧

i_iso:= make_z_iso' i Hi: z_iso x₁ x₂

p: # F g = h · # F i
C₁ ⟦ w, x₁ ⟧
 exact (g · inv_from_z_iso i_iso).
    
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂: C₁
i: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hi: is_z_isomorphism i
i_iso:= make_z_iso' i Hi: z_iso x₁ x₂
w: C₁
g: C₁ ⟦ w, x₂ ⟧
h: C₂ ⟦ F w, F x₁ ⟧
p: # F g = h · # F i
# F (g · inv_from_z_iso i_iso) = h
 abstract
        (rewrite functor_comp ;
         rewrite p ;
         rewrite !assoc' ;
         rewrite <- functor_comp ;
         etrans ;
           [ do 2 apply maponpaths ;
             exact (z_iso_inv_after_z_iso i_iso)
           | ] ;
         rewrite functor_id ;
         apply id_right).
    
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂: C₁
i: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hi: is_z_isomorphism i
i_iso:= make_z_iso' i Hi: z_iso x₁ x₂
w: C₁
g: C₁ ⟦ w, x₂ ⟧
h: C₂ ⟦ F w, F x₁ ⟧
p: # F g = h · # F i
(λ _ : # F (g · inv_from_z_iso i_iso) = h,
 g · inv_from_z_iso i_iso · i = g)
  (z_iso_is_cartesian_sfib_subproof0 C₁ C₂ F x₁ x₂ i
     Hi w g h p)
 abstract
        (cbn ;
         rewrite !assoc' ;
         refine (_ @ id_right _) ;
         apply maponpaths ;
         apply z_iso_after_z_iso_inv).
Defined.

Section CompositionCartesian.
  Context {C₁ C₂ : category}
          (F : C₁ ⟶ C₂)
          {x₁ x₂ x₃ : C₁}
          {f : x₁ --> x₂}
          (Hf : is_cartesian_sfib F f)
          {g : x₂ --> x₃}
          (Hg : is_cartesian_sfib F g).

  Section Factorization.
    Context {w : C₁}
            {h₁ : w --> x₃}
            {h₂ : F w --> F x₁}
            (p : # F h₁ = h₂ · # F (f · g)).

    
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_cartesian_sfib F f
g: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
Hg: is_cartesian_sfib F g
w: C₁
h₁: C₁ ⟦ w, x₃ ⟧
h₂: C₂ ⟦ F w, F x₁ ⟧
p: # F h₁ = h₂ · # F (f · g)
C₁ ⟦ w, x₂ ⟧

    
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_cartesian_sfib F f
g: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
Hg: is_cartesian_sfib F g
w: C₁
h₁: C₁ ⟦ w, x₃ ⟧
h₂: C₂ ⟦ F w, F x₁ ⟧
p: # F h₁ = h₂ · # F (f · g)
C₁ ⟦ w, x₂ ⟧

      
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_cartesian_sfib F f
g: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
Hg: is_cartesian_sfib F g
w: C₁
h₁: C₁ ⟦ w, x₃ ⟧
h₂: C₂ ⟦ F w, F x₁ ⟧
p: # F h₁ = h₂ · # F (f · g)
# F h₁ = h₂ · # F f · # F g

      abstract
        (refine (p @ _) ;
         rewrite functor_comp ;
         rewrite assoc ;
         apply idpath).
    Defined.

cartesian_factorization_sfib F Hf
  (cartesian_factorization_sfib F Hg h₁ (h₂ · # F f)
     comp_is_cartesian_sfib_factor_help_subproof) h₂
  (cartesian_factorization_sfib_over F Hg h₁
     (h₂ · # F f)
     comp_is_cartesian_sfib_factor_help_subproof)
· (f · g) = h₁

  (cartesian_factorization_sfib F Hg h₁ (h₂ · # F f)
     comp_is_cartesian_sfib_factor_help_subproof) h₂
  (cartesian_factorization_sfib_over F Hg h₁
     (h₂ · # F f)
     comp_is_cartesian_sfib_factor_help_subproof) · f
· g = h₁

h₁: C₁ ⟦ w, x₃ ⟧
h₂: C₂ ⟦ F w, F x₁ ⟧
p: # F h₁ = h₂ · # F (f · g)
h₁ = h₁

      apply idpath.
    Qed.

    
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_cartesian_sfib F f
g: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
Hg: is_cartesian_sfib F g
w: C₁
h₁: C₁ ⟦ w, x₃ ⟧
h₂: C₂ ⟦ F w, F x₁ ⟧
p: # F h₁ = h₂ · # F (f · g)
isaprop
  (∑ φ : C₁ ⟦ w, x₁ ⟧, # F φ = h₂ × φ · (f · g) = h₁)

Hf: is_cartesian_sfib F f
g: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
Hg: is_cartesian_sfib F g
w: C₁
h₁: C₁ ⟦ w, x₃ ⟧
h₂: C₂ ⟦ F w, F x₁ ⟧
p: # F h₁ = h₂ · # F (f · g)
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ φ : C₁ ⟦ w, x₁ ⟧, # F φ = h₂ × φ · (f · g) = h₁
pr1 φ₁ · (f · g) = h₁

          apply (pr22 φ₁).
        
C₁, C₂: category

x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁

comp_is_cartesian_sfib_factor_help · g = h₁
 apply cartesian_factorization_sfib_commute.

          apply idpath.

 apply cartesian_factorization_sfib_over.

pr1 φ₂ · (f · g) = h₁

          apply (pr22 φ₂).
        
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁

h₂: C₂ ⟦ F w, F x₁ ⟧

φ₁, φ₂: ∑ φ : C₁ ⟦ w, x₁ ⟧, # F φ = h₂ × φ · (f · g) = h₁
comp_is_cartesian_sfib_factor_help · g = h₁
 apply cartesian_factorization_sfib_commute.
    Qed.
  End Factorization.

  
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_cartesian_sfib F f
g: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
Hg: is_cartesian_sfib F g
is_cartesian_sfib F (f · g)

p: # F h₁ = h₂ · # F (f · g)
∃! φ : C₁ ⟦ w, x₁ ⟧, # F φ = h₂ × φ · (f · g) = h₁

  (∑ φ : C₁ ⟦ w, x₁ ⟧, # F φ = h₂ × φ · (f · g) = h₁)

# F ?pr1 = h₂
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_cartesian_sfib F f
g: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧

w: C₁

h₂: C₂ ⟦ F w, F x₁ ⟧
p: # F h₁ = h₂ · # F (f · g)
(λ _ : # F ?pr1 = h₂, ?pr1 · (f · g) = h₁) ?pr10

      
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_cartesian_sfib F f
g: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
Hg: is_cartesian_sfib F g
w: C₁
h₁: C₁ ⟦ w, x₃ ⟧
h₂: C₂ ⟦ F w, F x₁ ⟧
p: # F h₁ = h₂ · # F (f · g)
C₁ ⟦ w, x₁ ⟧
 exact (comp_is_cartesian_sfib_factor p).
      
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_cartesian_sfib F f
g: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
Hg: is_cartesian_sfib F g
w: C₁
h₁: C₁ ⟦ w, x₃ ⟧
h₂: C₂ ⟦ F w, F x₁ ⟧
p: # F h₁ = h₂ · # F (f · g)
# F (comp_is_cartesian_sfib_factor p) = h₂
 exact (comp_is_cartesian_sfib_factor_over p).
      
C₁, C₂: category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
Hf: is_cartesian_sfib F f
g: C₁ ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
Hg: is_cartesian_sfib F g
w: C₁
h₁: C₁ ⟦ w, x₃ ⟧
h₂: C₂ ⟦ F w, F x₁ ⟧
p: # F h₁ = h₂ · # F (f · g)
(λ _ : # F (comp_is_cartesian_sfib_factor p) = h₂,
 comp_is_cartesian_sfib_factor p · (f · g) = h₁)
  (comp_is_cartesian_sfib_factor_over p)
 exact (comp_is_cartesian_sfib_factor_comm p).
  Defined.
End CompositionCartesian.
